Carrying no more than soap and a few coins, the mysterious woman began knocking on doors, calling herself Princess Caraboo.

Madeline, a lovely name with a soft and delicate image ,is an old-fashioned favorite that returned to favor in the 1990's, combining a classic pedigree with a cute nickname option: Maddy. Madeline has been found frequently in literature, from the poems of Keats and Tennyson to Dickens' Nicholas Nickleby to the charming and much loved children's books of Ludwig Bemelmans starring the sprightly French schoolgirl. The name can be found in several spellings, including the French Madeleine and the non-classic Madelyn and Madalyn.
